| **Holistic per-run Postgres round-trip SUM is O(1) in scan/candle count + every batched/persist SQL uses FIXED parameterized text (R4-F2-batch6-c5, REQ-PERF-020)** | Aggregate read/write queries are batched (`symbol=ANY($1)` + `BETWEEN`, §3.8) so the per-run round-trip SUM does not scale with candle/scan count; the ranking persist uses UNNEST **array binding** (not inline `VALUES`), `executemany` (one prepared statement), and `copy_records_to_table` (COPY) — NO string-interpolated `IN`-lists — so asyncpg's prepared-statement cache holds a small bounded set and never thrashes across a sweep | (a) Assert aggregate query count is O(1) in scan count (independent of candle count); (b) assert the **prepared-statement cache size stays bounded across a multi-K sweep** (statement text invariant to K) |

---

# 12. Technology Decisions

## 12.1 Accelerator stack (versions + licenses + alternatives)

| Tech | Version floor/ceiling | License | Role | Alternative (and why not) |
|------|----------------------|---------|------|---------------------------|
| **numba** | `>=0.61,<0.67` | BSD-2-Clause | `@njit` per-candle kernel (P4) | Cython (build-step heavy, no transparent fallback); pure-Python (the fallback of record — kept). |
| **llvmlite** | `>=0.44,<0.48` | BSD-2-Clause | numba's LLVM backend (coupled ABI) | n/a — pinned single resolution (REQ-DEP-002). |
| **pyarrow** | `>=16,<21` | Apache-2.0 | Arrow hot frame + Feather V2 mmap + Parquet I/O (P5) | fastparquet (fewer pushdown stats, no Arrow zero-copy). |
| **duckdb** | `>=1.0,<2` | MIT | Parquet read engine w/ predicate+partition pushdown (P5) | Polars `scan_parquet` (kept as the alternate reader behind `KlineStore`; cross-engine byte-parity asserted REQ-STORE-023). |
| **Parquet** (format) | v2.x | Apache-2.0 | Immutable columnar sealed store | Feather/Arrow IPC (used for the mmap hot tier; Parquet for durable month files — different jobs). |

All four are the **optional `accel` extra**, import-guarded, with a pure-Python/Postgres fallback of record (ADR-005). The exact versions live in a hash-pinned lockfile; numba+llvmlite carry floor+ceiling for the coupled JIT ABI; the stack must not downgrade numpy below pandas' transitive floor (REQ-DEP-002).

## 12.2 Why these and not a framework

vectorbt / nautilus_trader / backtrader were evaluated and rejected for the engine (ADR-001): none model shared-capital cross-sectional portfolios with leverage/liquidation/funding + the portfolio-level equity cascade, so each would collapse to `@njit` callbacks through a foreign abstraction whose parity we'd have to re-prove. We write the numba kernel directly against our own oracle.

## 12.3 Testing tools per layer

| Layer | Tool | What it gates |
|-------|------|---------------|
| Engine parity (5m no-drill) | **Stored-snapshot golden master** (`test_backtest_golden.py` extended) | Byte-identical trades + equity_curve (replaces brittle magic numbers — discovery §7). |
| Float vs Decimal | **Differential float64-vs-Decimal harness** | SoA/numba float path within tolerance + non-optimistic vs the Decimal oracle (§3.7). |
| Drill / portfolio | **Two-sided sandwich property test** (Hypothesis-style) | drilled PnL ≤ always-LTF oracle AND ≥ coarse pessimistic bound (REQ-DRILL-018). |
| Merge-walk equivalence | **Boundary + randomized timeline property tests** | Same bar set per `[current, next_scan)`; epoch-OR-datetime; empty/single/before-first/after-last (REQ-ENG-002/005/006). |
| Cache | **Mock-client `call_count`** | Sealed day fetched once; rerun 0 Bybit calls (REQ-CACHE). |
| Storage tiers | **Cross-engine byte-parity** (DuckDB/Polars/pyarrow) + EXPLAIN plan-assertion | Identical int64/float64 arrays; partition pruning (REQ-STORE-023/013). |
| Migration | **Fresh-DB-vs-upgraded schema diff** + clone-rehearsal + post-apply-noop + **live-drift gate** + **version-int guard** + **populated-columns canary** | 0→58 ≡ 57→58; idempotency on the real target (REQ-MIG-040/041); committed golden schema snapshot diffed against live introspection post-v58 fails on drift, asserts ON-CONFLICT targets + COALESCE-over-NULL analytics on a mixed pre/post-v58 population (REQ-MIG-039, R1-F20); CI fails any duplicate/non-strictly-increasing version int or in-place edit of a released migration (REQ-MIG-002, R1-F21); canary asserts additive columns are POPULATED non-null after a run (REQ-OBS-044). |
| Migration import isolation | **CLI-vs-boot-once + accel-absent import test** | `migrate` entrypoint imports only the persistence/DDL layer; runs on the lean pure-Python image with numba/pyarrow/duckdb force-absent (REQ-MIG-029, R1-F22). |
| Backfill safety | **Concurrent-live-upserts-during-backfill no-deadlock test** | `SealBackfillRunner` chunked commits + short `lock_timeout`+retry never deadlock the live `_update_coverage` upserts (REQ-MIG-030/031, R1-F3 mig). |
| Dependencies | **CI matrix simulating each module absent** | `backend.main` imports; canonical run pure-Python; flag toggles to Postgres-identical (REQ-DEP-001/004). |
| Performance | **Benchmark regression gate** | Latency budgets §11.1–11.3 (hard: <10s numba / ≤90s HEAVY pure-Python wall); throughput floors §11.2 — **150k/s pure-Python is a hard gate; the 5M/s numba floor is the POST-P3-CALIBRATED regression tripwire (R4-F3-batch6-c4), not a pre-profiling absolute**; frozen-P0 ≥100× headline (baseline captured per §11.1 timeout-disabled protocol, R4-F8-batch6-c4). |
| API contract | **Result-JSON contract test** | `metrics.total_trades` + ~45 keys present/typed; no rename/remove (REQ-FE/API). |
| Profile / denylist gate (R2-F20-batch4) | **cProfile/py-spy artifact + hot-path denylist** | Each canonical-fixture run emits a profile artifact; a **denylist gate** fails CI if a forbidden call (per-bar `datetime`, numpy `__getitem__` in the hot loop, per-row DB insert, Decimal in the float lane) appears in the engine hot path (REQ-OBS-019/020). |
| Canary-defect battery + mutation (R2-F20-batch4) | **Enumerated injected-defect suite + mutation testing** | An enumerated battery injects known parity defects (off-by-one qty_step floor, reordered cascade, pairwise Σ-uPnL, swapped TP/SL, dropped funding tick) and asserts the golden/differential gates CATCH each; mutation testing on the kernel asserts the parity suite kills mutants (REQ-TEST-017/018). |
| Requirement traceability (R2-F20-batch4) | **REQ-ID → executing-test matrix** | A generated matrix maps every REQ-ID to the test(s) that execute it; CI fails on any REQ with zero executing tests — the gate that catches orphaned reqs (e.g. the PERF-019/023/028/033/042/043/045 owners, R2-F5-batch4) before merge (REQ-TEST-040). |
| Engine-lane lockstep (R2-F12-batch5) | **Pure-Python-vs-numba bit-identical, STANDING job** | The pure-Python lane (native list/memoryview data access) and the numba lane (direct numpy) are TWO implementations of the shared decision logic; a **standing CI job** (not a one-time P4 check) asserts both lanes produce bit-identical discrete fields + within-epsilon money on the golden fixture, so a parity drift between lanes is caught continuously (REQ-PAR-018, §3.4). |
| SSOT formula-level differential (R2-F2-batch5) | **Kernel-formula vs `trading_rules.py` property test** | An unconditional differential drives each re-implemented kernel formula (sizing/TP/SL/liq/fee/funding) vs its `trading_rules.py` helper over a randomized input grid (price, qty_step, leverage, capital_pct, funding sign), catching a divergent FORMULA the constant-equality guard cannot (REQ-PAR-016, §3.4). |
| Derived-coarse parity + rollback (R3-F3/R3-F4-batch2) | **Derived-vs-native-coarse equivalence gate + `BT_DERIVE_COARSE`-OFF native-1h byte-identical test** | For any coarse `simulation_interval`, derived-from-5m == legacy native-coarse (byte-identical Decimal lane / pinned-ε float lane, REQ-TEST-030); flag OFF reverts to the legacy native per-interval fetch/load path byte-identically (REQ-ROLL-015, §4.3/§7.2). |
| Frontend | `npx tsc --noEmit` + render-path test | `BacktestResultsPage.tsx:255` never hits the no-trades fallback on a real run. |

# Requirements Coverage Map

Every requirement CATEGORY (15 total, 517 reqs) → the component(s) that own it. No category is orphaned; phase tags reference the 7-phase rollout.

| Category | Count | Owning component(s) | Primary section(s) | Phase |
|----------|-------|---------------------|--------------------|-------|
| **PAR** — Parity-Correctness | 45 | `GoldenMasterOracle` (§3.7) + `BacktestEngine`/`engine_kernel` (§3.4) frozen semantics; `trading_rules.py` SSOT untouched | Prime Directive table, ADR-001, ADR-004, §3.7, §12.3 | P0 (gates all) |
| **CACHE** — Cache | 50 | `SealedManifest` (§3.2) + `KlineCacheService` [MODIFIED] (§3.8) | ADR-003, §4.1–4.2, §6.1, §9.2, R7/R8 | P1 |
| **ENG** — Engine | 34 | `SoADatasetBuilder` (§3.3) + `engine_kernel` (§3.4); `_evaluate_candles_until` rewrite (§3.8) | ADR-004, §3.3–3.4, §11.2, R14, §12.3 | P3/P4 |
| **STORE** — Storage | 45 | `KlineStore` (§3.1) + `SealedManifest` (§3.2) + Parquet/Feather layout (§4.3) | ADR-002/003, §4.1/4.3, §7.4, §11.4, R2–R6/R11–R13 | P1/P2/P3/P5 |
| **DRILL** — Drilldown | 23 | `DrilldownLoader` (§3.5) + `engine_kernel` coarse-extreme rules | ADR-001, §3.5, §6.3, R9, §12.3 | P0/P2/P3 |
| **SWEEP** — Sweep | 19 | `SweepRunner` (§3.6) + `SoADatasetBuilder` shared substrate; `sweep_tools.py`/`sweep_repo.py` | §3.6, §11.3 | P2/P6 |
| **PERF** — Performance | 45 | Per-REQ owner table below (NOT "owned by §11 (all)" — R1-F9): `PreflightEstimator` (§3.9), `KlineStore` streaming+tiers (§3.1), `SoADatasetBuilder` (§3.3), `engine_kernel` (§3.4), `SweepRunner` (§3.6), §7.4 CPU/RSS budgets, §9.5 loop-lag SLI, §11 budgets | §3.1/3.3/3.4/3.6/3.9, §7.4, §9.1/9.4/9.5, §11 (all) | cross / P3-P6 |
| **MIG** — Migration | 43 | `_seal_manifest_v58` callable (§4.4) + migration runner (`async_persistence.py`) | §4.4, §8.3, R11, §12.3 | P1 |
| **DEP** — Dependencies | 32 | Import guards `HAS_NUMBA/PYARROW/DUCKDB` + optional `accel` extra + lockfile | ADR-005, §7.1, §8.1, R1, §12.1 | P4/P5 |
| **ROLL** — Rollback | 34 | Master **`BACKTEST_SAFE_MODE`** + DB-backed `bt_flag_config` store owned by `CapabilityResolver` (§7.2, REQ-ROLL-001/002/003/004) + per-optimization feature flags (§7.2) + independent phase deploy (§7.3) + **admin/maintenance + DR surface** (§3.12, REQ-ROLL-024/025/030/032/033) + CD promotion guard + restore-point (§7.3, REQ-ROLL-007/028/029) | ADR-002/005, §7.2–7.3, §3.12, §10 (fallbacks) | cross |
| **OBS** — Observability | 49 | Structured-log counters/timers + parity-diff + pre-flight telemetry + invariant checks + **migration/deploy + storage-health alerting (§9.7)** | §9 (all incl. §9.7), §11.5 | cross |
| **TEST** — Testing | 44 | `GoldenMasterOracle` (§3.7) + differential/sandwich/property/benchmark/contract suites | §3.7, §12.3, Prime Directive | P0 (gates all) |
| **API** — API-Lifecycle | 24 | `BacktestService` [UNCHANGED-CONTRACT] (§3.8) + routers; result-JSON contract test; **terminal-state CAS + same-run_id single-flight (§5.5, REQ-API-012/015, R4-F11-batch6-c3)** | §5 (all), §5.5, R10 | cross |
| **CFG** — Config-Surface | 14 | `BacktestEngine` `config.get(...)` parity (§3.8) + `BacktestCreateRequest`/MCP `backtest_run` 1:1 | §5.1, ADR-001, Prime Directive | cross |
| **FE** — Frontend-Compat | 16 | Result/Trade JSON contract preservation (§5.2) — `metrics.total_trades` invariant | §5.2–5.3, §12.3 (frontend row) | cross |
| **TOTAL** | **517** | — | — | P0–P6 |

**Orphan check:** all 15 categories from `specs/backtest-optimization-requirements.md` (PAR 45, CACHE 50, ENG 34, STORE 45, DRILL 23, SWEEP 19, PERF 45, MIG 43, DEP 32, ROLL 34, OBS 49, TEST 44, API 24, CFG 14, FE 16 = **517**) are assigned to at least one owning component above. Cross-cutting categories (PERF/OBS/ROLL/API/CFG/FE) are owned by named components, not left implicit.

**PERF per-REQ owner table (R1-F9 — "present in a requirements file" ≠ "addressed in the architecture").** The previously-unaddressed PERF reqs now each name an owning component + design paragraph (the body cites PERF-034..040 explicitly; this table covers the rest):

| REQ-PERF | Owner / design paragraph |
|----------|--------------------------|
| 007 (vectorized scan-anchor pre-bind) | `SoADatasetBuilder` global-timeline + `searchsorted` anchor binding (§3.3, ADR-004) |
| 019 (B&H concurrent fetch — no serial blocking) | `backtest_service._attach_buy_hold` routes through `KlineStore` and fetches the B&H BTC series **concurrently** with the main load (not a serial post-step), §3.8 aux-kline reroute (R2-F5-batch1) |
| 023 (cold-ingest parse O(candles), no quadratic) | `KlineStore` columnar build parses each candle once into typed arrays — `O(candles)` ingest, no per-row re-scan; §3.1/§4.3 |
| 009 (O(1)-amortized ScanContext/regime) | `engine_kernel` incremental counters; no per-scan rebuild (§3.4) |
| 010 (turnover-linear, no O(closes²) history rescan) | `engine_kernel` O(1) adaptive-blacklist counters (§3.4 lowering plan) |
| 011 (native-seq hot loop, no element-wise numpy) | `engine_kernel` pure-Python lane materializes list/memoryview at chunk entry (§3.4, §11.2 floor) |
| 013 (cgroup-derived ceilings / multi-worker uvicorn) | §7.4 CPU/thread budget (cgroup quota, not `os.cpu_count`) |
| 014 (build-time peak ≤~1.5× final SoA) | `KlineStore.iter_klines_streamed` releases Records as consumed (§3.1, §7.4) |
| 015 (server-side cursor / bounded fetch) | `KlineStore.iter_klines_streamed` streaming seam (§3.1) |
| 016/017/018 (batched signals/trades/instrument fan-out) | `backtest_service` batched `ANY($1)` load + `executemany`/`COPY` persist (§3.8, §5.2, §11.6) |
| 021 (pool pre-warm / max_size) | `SweepRunner` parent-side pool provisioning (§3.6) |
| 024/025/029/030 (CPU budget / lock-free / GIL-yield / loop reserve) | §7.4 CPU/thread budget + §9.5 loop-lag SLI |
| 026/027 (per-combo result release / sweep GC) | `SweepRunner` persist-then-release + GC tune (§3.6) |
| 031 (live-fetch latency vs baseline during backfill) | §9.5 `live_scanner_fetch_latency_p95` SLI; `SealBackfillRunner` throttle (§3.10) |
| 032 (persist budget <3s) | §11.6 batched persistence |
| 034 (paginated trades latency flat) | §5.1 `GET /backtest/{id}/trades` index-backed cursor |
| 036 (≤2% counters overhead) | §9 O(trades+signals) instrumentation |
| 037/038/039 (admission / ±50% bracket / RSS reject-or-stream) | `PreflightEstimator` (§3.9) + RSS watchdog (§7.4) |
| 040 (JIT warm amortized) | `engine_kernel` jit_compile_ms (§3.4, §9.3) |
| 044 (degenerate-run short-circuit <100ms) | `SoADatasetBuilder` early-out (§3.3) |
| 022 (concurrent columnar+PG stitched read) | `KlineStore` generation-token snapshot contract (§3.1 parity) |
| 028 (optimize_config E2E budget + batched sweep persist) | `SweepRunner` end-to-end budget (baseline+sweep+rank under a documented wall) + single **fixed-text array-bound** `UPDATE` (UNNEST id+rank arrays, PERF-020-safe — NOT inline `VALUES`) batched persist (§3.6, REQ-SWEEP-009) |
| 020 (holistic round-trip SUM O(1) + fixed parameterized text / no cache thrash) | §3.8/§11.6 — aggregate queries O(1) in scan count; ranking persist uses UNNEST array binding + `executemany` + COPY, no string-interpolated `IN`-lists; prepared-statement-cache-bounded-across-multi-K-sweep test (R4-F2-batch6-c5) |
| 041 (per-run allocation release on complete/timeout-kill/cancel + no-leak soak) | `BacktestService` run-finalizer + `SweepRunner` — `finally`-scoped release of SoA arrays, position book, 1m drill memo, mmap/shared_memory segments, per-tier reader conns on EVERY terminal path; soak test over N heterogeneous runs (incl. killed+cancelled) asserts flat RSS, FD/mmap/shm/conn counts return to baseline, next-run-after-kill meets nominal budget (R4-F3-batch6-c5, §3.6 lifecycle) |
| 033 (metrics O(curve+trades), NO O(n²) drawdown) | `backtest_metrics` single-pass running-max drawdown/run-up + O(trades) reductions — no nested rescan (§5.2, REQ-PERF-033); a gate asserts metrics time scales linearly, not quadratically, in curve length |
| 042 (fallback-lane perf gate) | The pure-Python + Postgres + sequential baseline lane has its OWN benchmark gate (`≤60s` canonical, §11.1 lane-split) so a flag-off/degraded run is still bounded, not unmeasured (§11.2, §12.3 Performance row) |
| 043 (per-tier read-latency micro-bench) | A micro-benchmark asserts per-tier read latency (Arrow hot < Feather mmap < Parquet < Postgres) so a tier regression is caught; owned by §11.4 storage-tier bench (§9.2 `kline_tier_hits`) |
| 045 (fast-path bounded memory) | The §3.4 vectorized first-touch fast-path streams its barrier scan in bounded chunks (no full-universe materialization), RSS bounded under §7.4; a test asserts fast-path peak RSS stays within the klines budget |

---

## Appendix A — Phase → Component → Key Requirements (build-order traceability)

| Phase | Components delivered | Headline reqs | Golden-master gate |
|-------|----------------------|---------------|--------------------|
| **P0** Golden-master harness | `GoldenMasterOracle` (§3.7) | PAR-*, TEST-*, three-way Σ reconciliation | Freezes the oracle; gates every later phase |
| **P1** Cache re-download fix | `SealedManifest` (§3.2), v58 DDL-only (§4.4), `SealBackfillRunner` (§3.10), `KlineCacheService` [MOD] | CACHE-*, STORE-001..011, MIG-* | Rerun `bybit_kline_calls == 0` on sealed range; byte-identical klines; schema_version→58 sub-second |
| **P2** Batched loaders + parallel sweeps | `KlineStore` seam (§3.1), `SweepRunner` (§3.6), `DrilldownLoader` (§3.5), `PreflightEstimator` (§3.9) | STORE-012..016, SWEEP-001..009, DRILL-020/023, PERF-037/038/039 | NO-OP guarantee + drill-on/off SELECTION identical |
| **P3** SoA + merge-walk engine | `SoADatasetBuilder` (§3.3), `_evaluate_candles_until` rewrite | ENG-001..007, STORE-017..019, PERF (150k/s) | Bit-identical on 5m no-drill; ±10% setup-vs-N test |
| **P4** numba JIT kernel | `engine_kernel` (§3.4, guarded) | DEP-*, ENG (5M/s), PERF-040 | Pure-Python vs JIT bit-identical; CI module-absent matrix |
| **P5** Parquet/DuckDB read layer | `KlineStore` tiers (§3.1), Parquet layout (§4.3) | STORE-020..040, DEP-003/004 | Columnar flag off → Postgres-identical; cross-engine byte-parity |
| **P6** Vectorized fast-path + prange sweeps | fast-path in `engine_kernel`, `SweepRunner` ProcessPool | SWEEP-002/006/008, ENG fast-path | Fast-path vs sequential-kernel oracle (two-sided sandwich) |

## Appendix B — Adversarial-review quick-answers

- **"Does the SoA rewrite change any decision?"** No — it changes price *location* (searchsorted/pointers), not the rule set. Proven byte-identical on the 5m no-drill path + boundary/randomized property tests (REQ-ENG-002/005, ADR-004).
- **"What if numba won't install on Py3.14.3?"** Backend still imports (optional extra, guarded), canonical backtest runs pure-Python, P3 alone meets "minutes" (D5, ADR-005, R1).
- **"What if a Parquet file rots?"** sha256 + row-count check invalidates+rebuilds from the Postgres SOR; seal never depended on the file (REQ-STORE-026/028, R2/R6).
- **"Can the migration corrupt prod or crash-loop a deploy?"** v58 is a callable (no `;`-split bug), **additive DDL ONLY — zero data backfill inline** (R1-F1); `schema_version` reaches 58 sub-second so the global migration advisory lock is never held for a long backfill. Sealing runs in the deferred `SealBackfillRunner` (§3.10) outside the migration txn/lock, chunked-commit + bounded `lock_timeout`, frontier+lifecycle predicate (not count-vs-expected), wrong-DB/read-only guarded by a committed DB-identity row (§4.4, §8.5, REQ-MIG-018/020/028/043).
- **"Will the frontend break?"** `metrics.total_trades` + all ~45 keys are contract-tested present/typed; only optional nullable keys added; the degenerate/empty run still returns `total_trades=0` present (§3.3, §5.2, REQ-FE/PERF-044).
- **"Could a sweep OOM the live process?"** Pre-flight **rejects** a WIDE run whose FINAL SoA exceeds the klines budget before it takes a slot (streaming bounds only the LOAD transient, not RUN-stage residency — R2-F2-batch1, §7.4); the **runtime RSS watchdog aborts before OOM**, RSS ≤1GB (re-derived to include book/curve/interpreter/live headroom), klines ≤150MB, load-stage transient ≤1.5× SoA enforced (REQ-PERF-014/037/039, R12, §7.4).
- **"Could a parallel sweep starve live order placement?"** No — the live-trading breaker stays a parent-side dispatch gate (workers also poll an IPC heartbeat); a sweep pauses/sheds under an open breaker and resumes when it clears, runs in its own pool (not the 3 live UI slots), and CPU/thread caps are cgroup-derived to avoid oversubscription (§3.6, §7.4, R17).

---

*End of architecture. Next: Step 4 (Spec) per `/new-feature`. This document is the architectural contract; the spec elaborates per-phase acceptance criteria against the 517 requirement IDs.*
